     1	/* 主应用布局 */
     2	import React, { useEffect } from 'react';
     3	import { AnimatePresence, motion } from 'framer-motion';
     4	import Sidebar from './Sidebar';
     5	import TopBar from './TopBar';
     6	import CommandPalette from '@/components/global/CommandPalette';
     7	import NotificationPanel from '@/components/global/NotificationPanel';
     8	import { AppProvider, useApp } from '@/contexts/AppContext';
     9	
    10	// 模块懒加载
    11	import ChatModule from '@/components/chat/ChatModule';
    12	import KnowledgeModule from '@/components/knowledge/KnowledgeModule';
    13	import ToolsModule from '@/components/tools/ToolsModule';
    14	import SettingsModule from '@/components/settings/SettingsModule';
    15	
    16	/* 内层布局 — 必须在 AppProvider 内部渲染 */
    17	function AppLayoutInner() {
    18	  const { activeModule, darkMode } = useApp();
    19	
    20	  // 模块映射在组件内定义，避免模块级 JSX 在 HMR 时引发的 context 竞态
    21	  const moduleMap: Record<string, React.ReactElement> = {
    22	    chat:      <ChatModule />,
    23	    knowledge: <KnowledgeModule />,
    24	    tools:     <ToolsModule />,
    25	    settings:  <SettingsModule />,
    26	  };
    27	
    28	  useEffect(() => {
    29	    if (darkMode) {
    30	      document.documentElement.classList.add('dark');
    31	    } else {
    32	      document.documentElement.classList.remove('dark');
    33	    }
    34	  }, [darkMode]);
    35	
    36	  return (
    37	    <div className="flex min-h-screen w-full deep-space">
    38	      <Sidebar />
    39	
    40	      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
    41	        <TopBar />
    42	
    43	        <main className="flex-1 min-h-0 overflow-hidden relative">
    44	          <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
    45	            <motion.div
    46	              key={activeModule}
    47	              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 6 }}
    48	              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
    49	              exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -6 }}
    50	              transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
    51	              className="absolute inset-0"
    52	            >
    53	              {moduleMap[activeModule] ?? <ChatModule />}
    54	            </motion.div>
    55	          </AnimatePresence>
    56	        </main>
    57	      </div>
    58	
    59	      {/* 全局浮层 */}
    60	      <CommandPalette />
    61	      <NotificationPanel />
    62	    </div>
    63	  );
    64	}
    65	
    66	/* 外层导出 — 自带 AppProvider，HMR 时 context 始终有效 */
    67	export default function AppLayout() {
    68	  return (
    69	    <AppProvider>
    70	      <AppLayoutInner />
    71	    </AppProvider>
    72	  );
    73	}

function ToolCallCard({ tc }: { tc: NonNullable<Message['toolCall']> }) {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
  const isRunning = tc.status === 'running';
  const isDone = tc.status === 'done';
  const isError = tc.status === 'error';

  return (
    <div className="mt-2 mb-1 rounded-xl overflow-hidden border"
      style={{
        background: isRunning ? 'rgba(6,182,212,0.04)' : isDone ? 'rgba(16,185,129,0.04)' : 'rgba(244,63,94,0.04)',
        borderColor: isRunning ? 'rgba(6,182,212,0.2)' : isDone ? 'rgba(16,185,129,0.2)' : 'rgba(244,63,94,0.2)',
      }}>
      <button onClick={() => !isRunning && setExpanded(v => !v)}
        className="w-full flex items-center gap-2.5 px-3 py-2.5 text-left">
        <div className={cn(
          'w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shrink-0',
          isRunning ? 'bg-cyan-500/15' : isDone ? 'bg-emerald-500/15' : 'bg-rose-500/15',
        )}>
          <Wrench className={cn('w-3.5 h-3.5',
            isRunning ? 'text-cyan-400 animate-spin' : isDone ? 'text-emerald-400' : 'text-rose-400'
          )} />
        </div>
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-200">{tc.toolIcon} {tc.toolName}</span>
            <span className={cn('text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-medium',
              isRunning ? 'bg-cyan-500/15 text-cyan-400' :
              isDone    ? 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-400' :
                          'bg-rose-500/15 text-rose-400')}>
              {isRunning ? '⏳ 执行中…' : isDone ? '✅ 完成' : '❌ 失败'}
            </span>
            {tc.duration && <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-600 ml-auto">{(tc.duration / 1000).toFixed(2)}s</span>}
          </div>
          {tc.input && (
            <p className="text-[11px] text-slate-500 mt-0.5 truncate">
              {Object.entries(tc.input).map(([k, v]) => `${k}: ${JSON.stringify(v)}`).join(' · ')}
            </p>
          )}
        </div>
        {!isRunning && (
          <ChevronRight className={cn('w-3.5 h-3.5 text-slate-600 transition-transform shrink-0', expanded && 'rotate-90')} />
        )}
      </button>
      <AnimatePresence>
        {expanded && tc.output && (
          <motion.div initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }} animate={{ height: 'auto', opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }} transition={{ duration: 0.18 }}
            className="overflow-hidden">
            <div className="px-3 pb-3 pt-0 border-t border-[var(--border-subtle)]">
              <p className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-medium mt-2 mb-1 uppercase tracking-wide">输出结果</p>
              <pre className="text-[11px] font-mono text-slate-300 whitespace-pre-wrap leading-relaxed bg-black/20 rounded-lg p-2.5">
                {JSON.stringify(tc.output, null, 2)}
              </pre>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ── 结构化卡片（card 类型） ─────────────────────────────────────────── */
const CARD_BADGE_COLORS: Record<string, string> = {
  cyan:    'bg-cyan-500/15 text-cyan-400 border-cyan-500/25',
  emerald: 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-400 border-emerald-500/25',
  violet:  'bg-violet-500/15 text-violet-400 border-violet-500/25',
  amber:   'bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-400 border-amber-500/25',
};

function StructuredCard({ data }: { data: CardData }) {
  return (
    <div className="mt-3 rounded-xl border border-[var(--border-subtle)] overflow-hidden"
      style={{ background: 'var(--surface-active)' }}>
      {/* 卡头 */}
      <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-[var(--border-subtle)] flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
        <div className="min-w-0">
          <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-100 text-balance">{data.title}</p>
          {data.subtitle && <p className="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-0.5 text-pretty">{data.subtitle}</p>}
        </div>
        {data.badge && (
          <span className={cn(
            'text-[10px] font-medium px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full border whitespace-nowrap shrink-0',
            CARD_BADGE_COLORS[data.badgeColor ?? 'cyan']
          )}>
            {data.badge}
          </span>
        )}
      </div>
      {/* 数据行 */}
      {data.rows && data.rows.length > 0 && (
        <div className="divide-y divide-[var(--border-subtle)]">
          {data.rows.map((row, i) => (
            <div key={i} className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2.5 gap-4">
              <span className="text-xs text-slate-500 shrink-0">{row.label}</span>
              <span className={cn(
                'text-xs font-medium text-right truncate',
                row.highlight ? 'aurora-text' : 'text-slate-200'
              )}>
                {row.value}
              </span>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
      {/* 操作按钮 */}
      {data.actions && data.actions.length > 0 && (
        <div className="px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2 border-t border-[var(--border-subtle)]">
          {data.actions.map((act, i) => (
            <button key={i} className={cn(
              'px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-xs font-medium transition-colors',
              act.variant === 'primary'
                ? 'btn-aurora text-white'

  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(defaultOpen ?? false);

/* ── AI 消息气泡 ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function AgentMessage({ msg, onRetry, onEdit }: {
  msg: Message;
  onRetry?: (id: string) => void;
  onEdit?: (id: string) => void;
}) {
  const agent = msg.agentId ? getAgent(msg.agentId) : null;
  const isStreaming = msg.status === 'streaming';
  const isError = msg.status === 'error';
  const contentType = msg.contentType ?? 'text';

  return (
    <div className="flex justify-start gap-3 max-w-[80%]">
      {agent && <AgentAvatar agentId={agent.id} />}

              boxShadow: isError
                ? '0 2px 8px rgba(244,63,94,0.10)'
                : `var(--shadow-sm), inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255,255,255,0.04)`,
            }}
          >
            {isError ? (
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-rose-400">
                <AlertCircle className="w-4 h-4 shrink-0" />
                <span className="text-xs">{msg.content || '生成失败，请重试'}</span>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <span className="whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm" style={{ color: 'var(--text-primary)' }}>
                {msg.content}
                {isStreaming && <StreamCursor />}
              </span>
            )}
          </div>
        )}

        {/* 代码块（streaming 时显示骨架） */}
        {contentType === 'code' && msg.codeBlock && (
          <CodeBlock data={msg.codeBlock} streaming={isStreaming && !msg.codeBlock.code} />
        )}

        {/* 图片 */}
        {contentType === 'image' && (
          <ImageMessage
            url={msg.imageUrl ?? ''}
            caption={msg.imageCaption}
            streaming={isStreaming}
          />

          <StructuredCard data={msg.cardData} />

        {!isStreaming && (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-1.5 px-1">
            {onRetry && (
              <button onClick={() => onRetry(msg.id)}
                className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[11px] text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-300 transition-colors">
                <RotateCcw className="w-3 h-3" />重试
              </button>
            )}
            {onEdit && msg.type === 'user' && (
              <button onClick={() => onEdit(msg.id)}
                className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[11px] text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-300 transition-colors">
                <Pencil className="w-3 h-3" />编辑
              </button>
            )}
            {msg.meta?.tokens && (
              <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-700 ml-auto">
                {msg.meta.tokens} tokens
                {msg.meta.durationMs ? ` · ${(msg.meta.durationMs / 1000).toFixed(1)}s` : ''}
              </span>
            )}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ── 审批消息 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function ApprovalMessage({ msg }: { msg: Message }) {
  const [status, setStatus] = useState<'pending' | 'approved' | 'rejected'>('pending');
  return (
    <div className="flex justify-start gap-3 max-w-[75%]">
      <AgentAvatar agentId={msg.agentId!} />
      <div>
        <AgentLabel agentId={msg.agentId!} time={msg.timestamp} />
        <div
          className="mt-1 px-4 py-3 rounded-2xl rounded-tl-sm text-sm text-slate-200 leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-line"
          style={{ background: 'rgba(245,158,11,0.08)', border: '1px solid rgba(245,158,11,0.25)' }}
        >
          {msg.content}
          {status === 'pending' ? (
            <div className="flex gap-2 mt-3">
              <button onClick={() => setStatus('approved')} className="px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-xs font-medium btn-aurora text-white">
                批准
              </button>
              <button onClick={() => setStatus('rejected')}
                className="px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-xs font-medium bg-rose-500/20 text-rose-400 border border-rose-500/30 hover:bg-rose-500/30 transition-colors">
                驳回
              </button>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className={cn('mt-3 text-xs font-medium', status === 'approved' ? 'text-emerald-400' : 'text-rose-400')}>
              {status === 'approved' ? '✅ 已批准' : '❌ 已驳回'}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ── 头像 & 标签 ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function AgentAvatar({ agentId }: { agentId: string }) {
  const agent = getAgent(agentId);
  if (!agent) return null;
  return (

function AgentAvatar({ agentId }: { agentId: string }) {
  const agent = getAgent(agentId);
  if (!agent) return null;
  return (
    <div
      className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-bold shrink-0 mt-1"
      style={{ background: `${agent.color}28`, border: `2px solid ${agent.color}55`, color: agent.color }}
    >
      {agent.avatar}
    </div>
  );
}

function AgentLabel({ agentId, time, meta }: { agentId: string; time: Date; meta?: Message['meta'] }) {
  const agent = getAgent(agentId);

        <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-white/5 border border-white/8 text-slate-600">{meta.model}</span>
      )}
      <span className="text-xs text-slate-700 ml-auto">{timeStr(time)}</span>
    </div>

/* ── 图片消息 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function ImageMessage({ url, caption, streaming }: { url: string; caption?: string; streaming?: boolean }) {
  const [loaded, setLoaded] = useState(false);
  if (streaming) {
    return (
      <div className="mt-3 rounded-xl overflow-hidden border border-[var(--border-subtle)] bg-black/20
        flex items-center justify-center h-32 gap-2 text-xs text-slate-500">
        <ImageIcon className="w-4 h-4 animate-pulse" />
        <span>图片生成中<StreamCursor /></span>
      </div>
    );
  }
  return (
    <div className="mt-3 space-y-1.5">
      <div className="rounded-xl overflow-hidden border border-[var(--border-subtle)] bg-black/20 relative">
        {!loaded && (
          <div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center">
            <div className="w-6 h-6 border-2 border-cyan-400/30 border-t-cyan-400 rounded-full animate-spin" />
          </div>
        )}
        <img
          src={url}
          alt={caption ?? '生成图片'}
          onLoad={() => setLoaded(true)}
          className={cn('w-full max-h-72 object-cover transition-opacity duration-300', loaded ? 'opacity-100' : 'opacity-0')}
        />
      </div>
      {caption && (
        <p className="text-xs text-slate-500 px-1">{caption}</p>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

                  <span className="text-xs font-mono text-rose-400/70 ml-auto">{recordSeconds}s</span>
                </div>
              </motion.div>
            )}
          </AnimatePresence>

          {/* 文本域 */}
          <textarea ref={textareaRef} value={text}
            onChange={e => handleTextChange(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
            onFocus={() => setFocused(true)}
            onBlur={() => setFocused(false)}
            rows={2}
            disabled={isStreaming}
            placeholder={recording ? '' : isStreaming ? '正在生成中，请稍候…' : '向 Acta 下达任务，输入 / 触发指令，Shift+Enter 换行…'}
            className={cn(
              'w-full bg-transparent text-sm text-slate-200 placeholder-slate-600 outline-none resize-none leading-relaxed',
              isStreaming && 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed'
            )}
          />

          {/* 底部工具栏 */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
              {/* 附件上传 */}
              <input ref={fileInputRef} type="file" multiple className="hidden" onChange={handleFileChange} />
              <button onClick={() => fileInputRef.current?.click()}
                className={cn('p-2 rounded-lg transition-colors', attachments.length > 0 ? 'text-violet-400 bg-violet-500/15' : 'text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300 hover:bg-white/8')}
                title="上传附件">
                <Paperclip className="w-4 h-4" />
              </button>

              {/* @提及 */}
              <button className="p-2 rounded-lg text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300 hover:bg-white/8 transition-colors" title="@提及">
                <AtSign className="w-4 h-4" />
              </button>

              {/* / 指令 */}
              <button onClick={() => { setText(t => t.endsWith('/') ? t : t + '/'); setSlashOpen(true); setSlashQuery(''); setTimeout(() => textareaRef.current?.focus(), 30); }}
                className={cn('p-2 rounded-lg transition-colors', slashOpen ? 'text-cyan-400 bg-cyan-500/15' : 'text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300 hover:bg-white/8')}
                title="快捷指令">
                <Slash className="w-4 h-4" />
              </button>

              {/* 技能 */}
              <button onClick={() => { setSkillPanelOpen(v => !v); setPromptPanelOpen(false); }}
                className={cn('p-2 rounded-lg transition-colors', skillPanelOpen ? 'text-cyan-400 bg-cyan-500/15' : 'text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300 hover:bg-white/8')}
                title="插入技能">
